    <h2>Home</h2> 
    <!-- Start Sidebar --> 
    <div id="sidebar"> 
     <div class="nav"> 
      <h3 class="accessibility">Main Navigation</h3>

       <li><a href="/directory.html" title="Our People">Our People</a></li>

       <li><a href="/dept.html" title="Our Departments">Our Departments</a></li>

    <!-- Start Content Area --> 
    <div id="main"> 
     <div id="omnicontent"> 
      <h3>An Integrated Approach</h3> 
      <p>The UC Riverside Office of Strategic Communications is responsible for creating integrated programs that publicize and support the university’s mission of teaching, research and service to audiences through first-person communication, programs and publications.</p> 
      <div id="box"> 
       <ul id="ul_puzzle"> 
        <li><a id="a_osc" title="Office of Strategic Communications" href="#tab_osc"> </a></li> 
        <li><a id="a_cds" title="Creative Design Services" href="#tab_cds"> </a></li> 
        <li><a id="a_marketing" title="Marketing" href="#tab_marketing"> </a></li> 
        <li><a id="a_media" title="Media Relations" href="#tab_media"> </a></li> 
        <li><a id="a_video" title="Video Production" href="#tab_video"> </a></li> 
        <li><a id="a_web" title="Web Development" href="#tab_web"> </a></li> 
       </ul> 
       <div id="tab_osc"> 
        <img class="border_image_top" src="/images/box/osc_ttl.gif" alt=" " width="504" height="72" /> 
        <h3 class="accessibility">How can Strategic Communications Help You?</h3> 
        <h4 class="accessibility">A Diverse Set of Marketing and Promotional Services for UC Riverside</h4> 
        <p><img id="big_puzzle" class="img_L_borderless_close" src="/images/box/big_puzzle.png" alt=" " width="177" height="161" /><strong>The departments within</strong> the Office of Strategic Communications work together to promote you and your university. <img id="yellow_puzzle" class="img_R_borderless_close" src="/images/box/yellow_puzzle.png" alt=" " width="123" height="99" />Browse the tabs to learn what we do and how we do it.</p> 
       </div> 
       <div id="tab_cds"> 
        <img class="border_image_top" src="/images/box/cds_ttl.gif" alt="" width="504" height="72" /> 
        <h3 class="accessibility">Creative Design Services</h3> 
        <h4 class="accessibility">A Diverse Set of Marketing and Promotional Services for UC Riverside</h4> 
        <p><strong><img id="cds_brochure" class="img_R_borderless_close" src="/images/box/cds_brochure.png" alt=" " width="164" height="167" />From conception to delivery</strong>, UCR’s award-winning in-house design team help colleges and departments produce communication projects that tell your story to the world.</p> 
        <p><a class="standout2" href="http://creativedesign.ucr.edu/">Visit the Creative Design Services site</a></p> 
       </div> 
       <div id="tab_marketing"> 
        <img class="border_image_top" src="/images/box/marketing_ttl.gif" alt=" " width="504" height="72" /> 
        <h3 class="accessibility">Marketing</h3> 
        <h4 class="accessibility">A Diverse Set of Marketing and Promotional Services for UC Riverside</h4> 
        <p><strong>From advertising to publications</strong>, creative development to market research, the Marketing team is responsible for developing and implementing integrated marketing strategies that enhance the university’s image and reputation.</p> 
        <p><a class="standout2" href="http://marketing.ucr.edu/">Visit the Marketing site</a></p> 
       </div> 
       <div id="tab_media"> 
        <img class="border_image_top" src="/images/box/media_ttl.gif" alt="" width="504" height="72" /> 
        <h3 class="accessibility">Media Relations</h3> 
        <h4 class="accessibility">A Diverse Set of Marketing and Promotional Services for UC Riverside</h4> 
        <p><strong>The Media Relations team</strong> communicates with media around the world to spread the news about what is happening at UC Riverside. They are also responsible for several publications, including <cite>UCR Magazine</cite> and <cite>Inside UCR</cite>.</p> 
        <p><a class="standout2" href="http://mediarelations.ucr.edu/">Visit the Media Relations site</a></p> 
       </div> 
       <div id="tab_video"> 
        <img class="border_image_top" src="/images/box/video_ttl.gif" alt=" " width="504" height="72" /> 
        <h3 class="accessibility">Video Production</h3> 
        <h4 class="accessibility">A Diverse Set of Marketing and Promotional Services for UC Riverside</h4> 
        <p><strong><img class="img_R_borderless_close" src="/images/box/video_image.png" alt=" " width="199" height="146" />UCR’s primary source for</strong> original video and television programming. Its facilities have full post-production capabilities and are a vast resource of the campus and the Inland Southern California community.</p> 
        <p><a class="standout2" href="http://videoproduction.ucr.edu/">Visit the Video Production site</a></p> 
       </div> 
       <div id="tab_web"> 
        <img class="border_image_top" src="/images/box/web_ttl.gif" alt=" " width="504" height="72" /> 
        <h3 class="accessibility">Web Development</h3> 
        <h4 class="accessibility">A Diverse Set of Marketing and Promotional Services for UC Riverside</h4> 
        <p><strong><img class="img_R_borderless_close" src="/images/box/web_dev_image.png" alt=" " width="157" height="163" />The Web Development team</strong> is responsible for the design and upkeep of the award-winning UCR “Umbrella” website as well as oversight of the university’s overall online presence.</p> 
        <p><a class="standout2" href="http://webdevelopment.ucr.edu/">Visit the Web Development site</a></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="divided3"> 
       <div class="column3"> 
        <h3><img id="ucr_mag" src="/images/ucr_mag_ttl.png" alt="UCR Magazine: Quarterly Publication" width="187" height="140" /></h3> 
        <p>Read the <a href="http://magazine.ucr.edu/">latest issue of our campus magazine</a>.</p> 
       </div> 
       <div class="column3"> 
        <h3><img id="inside_ucr" src="/images/inside_ucr_ttl.png" alt="Inside UCR: Bi-Monthly Publication" width="187" height="140" /></h3> 
        <p>See the <a href="http://ucrtoday.ucr.edu/inside-ucr">latest on-campus news</a> with our in-house newspaper.</p> 
       </div> 
       <div class="column3R"> 
        <h3><img id="ucr_youtube" src="/images/ucr_youtube_ttl.png" alt="UCR on YouTube" width="186" height="124" /></h3> 
        <p>View the <a class="external" title="external site: YouTube" href="http://www.youtube.com/ucriverside">UC Riverside channel</a> on YouTube.</p> 
       </div> 
       <div class="clear"></div> 
      </div> 
      <h3><img src="/images/media_training_ttl.gif" alt="Media Training" width="167" height="38" /></h3> 
      <p>Want some <a href="http://mediarelations.ucr.edu/training.html">pointers about upcoming interviews</a> with the media? Our public information officers are here to help.</p> 
      <h3 class="section"><img src="/images/portrait_scheduler_ttl.png" alt="Portrait Scheduler" width="209" height="35" /></h3> 
      <p>The Video Production Unit can take professional-quality head shots of UCR faculty for both university and personal use. <a href="/cgi-bin/photo/schedule.cgi">Visit the Portrait Scheduler</a> to schedule an appointment.</p> 
      <h3 class="section"><img src="/images/identity_standards_manual_ttl.gif" alt="Identity Standars Manual" width="263" height="38" /></h3> 
      <p>The <a href="http://creativedesign.ucr.edu/ism/">Identity Standards Manual</a> will ensure that your communications materials adhere to the campus’ brand standards to facilitate smooth project development.</p> 
      <h3 class="section"><img src="/images/ucr_web_toolbox_ttl.gif" alt="UCR Web Toolbox" width="182" height="45" /></h3> 
      <p>A list of resources that can help you build and maintain a great website.</p> 
      <h3 class="section"><img src="/images/ibooks_guide_ttle.png" alt="UCR iBooks Guide" width="190" height="45" /></h3> 
      <p>Want to view your favorite UCR Publications on your iPad? Check out our <a href="/ibooks/">ibooks guide</a> to learn how.</p> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <!-- End Content Area -->

   <h1><a href="//www.ucr.edu/"><span class="printonly">UC Riverside</span></a></h1> 
   <div class="pagewrapper"> 
    <div id="search"> 
     <div id="nav_utility"> 
      <ul>

    <div id="main"> 
     <iframe class="top" title="UCR Location from Google Maps" width="484" height="400" frameborder="0" scrolling="no" marginheight="0" marginwidth="0" src="https://maps.google.com/maps?f=d&amp;source=embed&amp;saddr=&amp;daddr=W+Campus+Dr+Parking+Kiosk&amp;hl=en&amp;geocode=FVtoBgIdh6cB-Q&amp;aq=0&amp;sll=33.973168,-117.331116&amp;sspn=0.006611,0.009645&amp;t=m&amp;mra=ls&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;ll=33.980449,-117.336731&amp;spn=0.028469,0.041456&amp;z=14&amp;iwloc=ddw1&amp;output=embed"></iframe> 
     <p class="notop"><a href="https://maps.google.com/maps?f=d&amp;source=embed&amp;saddr=&amp;daddr=W+Campus+Dr+Parking+Kiosk&amp;hl=en&amp;geocode=FVtoBgIdh6cB-Q&amp;aq=0&amp;sll=33.973168,-117.331116&amp;sspn=0.006611,0.009645&amp;t=m&amp;mra=ls&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;ll=33.980449,-117.336731&amp;spn=0.028469,0.041456&amp;z=14&amp;iwloc=ddw1">View Larger Map</a></p> 
     <div class="column23"> 
      <h3>Basic Directions to UC Riverside</h3> 
      <h4>From Los Angeles County</h4> 
      <p><strong>From the 91 Freeway: </strong>Take CA-91 east to the CA-60 east. Exit at University Avenue and turn left. At the second light, take a right onto West Campus Drive.</p> 
      <p><strong>From the 10 Freeway:</strong> Take the I-10 east to the I-15 south and then to CA-60 east. Exit at University Avenue and turn left. At the second light, take a right onto West Campus Drive.</p> 
      <p><strong>From the 60 Freeway:</strong> Take the CA-60 east. Exit at University Avenue and turn left. At the second light, take a right onto West Campus Drive.</p> 
      <h4>From Ontario Airport</h4> 
      <p><strong>From the 10 Freeway:</strong> Take the I-10 east, to the I-15 south and then to the CA-60 east. Exit at University Avenue and turn left. At the second light, take a right onto West Campus Drive.</p> 
      <p><strong>From the 60 Freeway:</strong> Take the CA-60 east. Exit at University Avenue and turn left. At the second light, take a right onto West Campus Drive.</p> 
      <h4>From Orange County</h4> 
      <p>Take the CA-91 east to the CA-60 east. Exit at University Avenue and turn left. At the second light, take a right onto West Campus Drive.</p> 
      <h4>From Palm Springs</h4> 
      <p>Take the I-10 west to CA-60 west. Exit at University Avenue and turn left. At the second light, take a right onto West Campus Drive.</p> 
      <h4>From San Bernardino </h4> 
      <p>Take the I-215 south to the CA-60 east. Exit at University Avenue and turn left. At the second light, take a right onto West Campus Drive.</p> 
      <h4> From San Diego County</h4> 
      <p>Take the I-15 north to the I-215 north to the CA-60 west. Exit at University Avenue and turn left. At the second light, take a right onto West Campus Drive.</p> 
     </div> 
     <div class="column3R on_the_side2"> 
      <h3>Parking, Traffic &amp; Campus Information</h3> 
      <h4>Printable Campus Map</h4> 
      <p><a href="http://www.campusmap.ucr.edu/map.pdf">Download an 8&frac12;&times;11 PDF UCR campus map.</a></p> 
      <h4>Online Campus Map</h4> 
      <p><a href="http://www.campusmap.ucr.edu/campusMap.php">Visit our online campus map.</a></p> 
      <h4>Visitor Parking</h4> 
      <p>University visitors may obtain parking permits at the Information Kiosk or self-service dispensers. Permits are valid in visitor lots or Gold parking zones. Zones are enforced 7 a.m. to 10 p.m., 7 days a week.</p> 
      <p>Every vehicle, unless otherwise exempt, must display a valid parking permit when parking on UCR property.</p> 
      <p>For more information on parking at UCR, <a href="http://parking.ucr.edu/visitor/kiosk.html">visit the Parking website.</a></p> 
      <h4>Traffic Information</h4> 
      <p><a class="external" title="external site: Sigalert.com" href="http://www.sigalert.com/Map.asp?Region=Greater+Los+Angeles#lat=34.00245&amp;lon=-117.36423&amp;z=2">Real-time traffic reports around UC Riverside</a> from Sigalert.com.</p> 
     </div>

              <h3 class="fw-b fz-s lh-115"><a class="" href="http://news.yahoo.com/anti-fracking-activist-barred-40-percent-pennsylvania-county-213256111--finance.html" data-ylk="sec:strm;cat:default;bpos:1;cpos:2;pkgt:4;slk:title;ct:1;rspns:nav;">Anti-fracking activist barred from visiting friends, grocery store</a></h3>
              <p class="summary mt-xxs">By David DeKok HARRISBURG, Pennsylvania (Reuters) - A court injunction obtained by Texas-based Cabot Oil &amp; Gas is preventing Pennsylvania resident Vera Scroggins from going to her local grocery store, her friends' homes, schools, or even the hospital. That's because those properties sit atop the more than 200,000 acres in Susquehanna County that the energy producer owns and leases for gas extraction - land on which Scroggins, a determined anti-fracking activist, is not allowed to tread. A judge in October granted Cabot's request to bar Scroggins from the land - more than 40 percent of Susquehanna County, where she lives - after her repeated trespassing, court documents show. Her offending actions included giving a tour last year to anti-drilling celebrities Susan Sarandon, Yoko Ono, and Sean Lennon, the documents said.</p>

    rtJSDone = Number(new Date());

    if ( "undefined" != typeof(rt_LogTime) ) { 
        rt_LogTime("t1", rtJSLoad - rtJSStart, true); 

        function DOMLoadedListener(){
            domContentLoaded = Number(new Date());
            rt_LogTime("t4", domContentLoaded - rtTop, true);
        }
        
        if(window.addEventListener){
            window.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", DOMLoadedListener, false);    
        }

        function settingRTTime(){
            rt_LogTime("t3", window.firstImageLoadTime - rtTop, true);
        }

        (function imageRoundTrip(rtWaitForImage){
            if(rtWaitForImage < 15){
                if(window.firstImageLoadTime){
                    settingRTTime();
                }else{
                    rtWaitForImage++;
                    setTimeout(function(){
                        imageRoundTrip(rtWaitForImage);
                    }, 100);
                }
            }
        })(0);
        
        (function(){
            if(!String.prototype.trim){
                String.prototype.trim = function (){
                    return this.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,'');
                };
            }

            cookieArrary = document.cookie.split(";");

            for(var j = 0; j < cookieArrary.length; j++){
                var rtCookie = cookieArrary[j].split('=')[0];
                rtCookie = rtCookie.trim();
                if(rtCookie == "RT"){
                    var unloadTime = cookieArrary[j].split('=')[2];
                    unloadTime = Number(unloadTime.substring(0, unloadTime.length - 2));
                    if(typeof unloadTime === "number"){
                        rt_LogTime("t2", rtTop - unloadTime , true);
                    }
                }
            }
        })();
    }

      <div id="about"> 
       <div class="texttab-column"> 
        <h5>Vision Statement</h5> 
        <p>The mission of the University of California Police Department, Riverside is to enhance the quality of life by providing a secure and safe environment through professional service to the University community.</p> 
        <h5>Mission Statement</h5> 
        <p>We of the University of California Police Department, Riverside recognize our contribution to the quality of life and a safe environment in our community through the provision of professional law enforcement services. We will meet the challenge of providing these services by basing our thoughts and actions on the following shared values.</p> 
        <h6>Service to Our Community</h6> 
        <p>We value the opportunity to provide service in a manner which is fair, courteous, responsive and efficient. An attitude of respect for, and the protection of, the worth, dignity and rights of all is the foundation of our law enforcement agency.</p> 
        <h6>Integrity</h6> 
        <p>We value candor, honesty and ethical behavior in members of our department. We are committed to uphold our positions of trust by maintaining the highest ethical standards as set forth in the Law Enforcement Code of Ethics.</p> 
        <h6>Responsibility and Accountability</h6> 
        <p>We value the need for effective use of our resources and to provide a spirit of openness in communications with our community. We will be responsible for our actions, willing to admit our mistakes and ensure that our behavior earns the support and trust of all segments of the public.</p> 
        <p>We have a long-standing practice of engaging the community stakeholders in its hiring and promotional processes. This input is normally obtained via a search committee membership that includes members from the <a href="http://www.ucr.edu/about/vc_affairs.html" target="_blank">Office of the Vice Chancellor for Student Affairs</a> who have frequent interaction with the police, students and staff.</p> 
        <h6>Professionalism</h6> 
        <p>We value professionalism by having a clear sense of commitment, perspective and direction. Professionalism is developed by creating an environment that encourages teamwork, innovation and constant evaluation of ourselves. A professional attitude is dedicated to quality, timeliness and excellence in our service to the community.</p> 
        <h6>Pride and Satisfaction in our Profession</h6> 
        <p>We believe our work to be a source of enjoyment and satisfaction. We are proud of our accomplishments as an integral part of the University community. We enjoy what we have chosen to do serving the law enforcement profession with the University of California Police Department, Riverside.</p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div id="letter"> 
       <div class="texttab-column"> 
        <p>Welcome to the official web site of the University of California Police Department, Riverside. The UCR Police Department was established in 1954 on this campus. The Police Department is a professional police agency staffed by individuals who cherish and preserve the highest standards of conduct and performance.</p> 
        <p>As Chief of Police, I am proud of this department and every member of the organization. Employees have showed continuing dedication and leadership in law enforcement through their own initiative. All members of the department are responsible for upholding this fine tradition.</p> 
        <p>The mission of the UCR Police Department is to heighten the quality of life by providing a secure and safe environment through professional service to the University community.</p> 
        <p style="text-align: justify;">Mike Lane<br />Chief of Police</p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div id="faq"> 
       <div class="texttab-column"> 
        <p><strong>Where can I report an anonymous tip? </strong><br />Go <a href="/anon.html">here</a>.</p> 
        <p><strong>I'm hosting an event. Does UCPD need to be involved?</strong> <br />Yes, please see the <a href="/faq/matrix.html">Special Event Staffing Matrix</a>.</p> 
        <p><strong>What is UC Riverside's skateboard and skate policy? </strong><br />It is currently under revision. As such, there is no official policy at this time.</p> 
        <p><strong>Does UCPD do Livescan fingerprinting? </strong><br />Yes, please see the<a href="/faq/livescan.html"> livescan webpage</a>.</p> 
        <p><strong>How do I recognize a suspicious package? What do I do if I suspect a mail bomb? </strong><br />Please see the <a href="/faq/mail.html">suspicious package checklist.</a></p> 
        <p><strong>Does UCPD have a lost and found? </strong><br />Yes, it may be accessed <a href="http://ucrlf.com/selectitemtype.aspx">here</a>.</p> 
        <p><strong>How do I obtain a police report? </strong><br />Please follow the instructions <a href="/faq/arrestreportsfaq.pdf" target="_blank">here</a>.</p> 
        <p><strong>What is the alarm system and 800 MHz service? </strong><br />Please refer to the systems <a href="/faq/alarm800mhzfaq.pdf" target="_blank">webpage</a>.</p> 
        <p><strong>How do I get involved with UCPD? </strong><br />Join the <a href="/cso/cso.html">Community Service Officer program</a>, leave <a href="/feedback.html">feedback</a>, or stop by UCPD's main branch to learn more.</p>

     <div class="boxed content" role="main"> 
      <h2>Web Security Start-up Receives $1.1 million</h2> 
      <p class="deck">Start-up co-founded by UC Riverside graduate and professor that helps web site owners prevent, detect and recover from hacker attacks has now officially launched</p> 
      <p class="byline">By <a href="http://ucrtoday.ucr.edu/author/snealon" title="View all posts by Sean Nealon" rel="author">Sean Nealon</a> on <em>February 17, 2012</em></p> 
      <div class="share"> 
       <p>Share this article: </p> 
       <ul class="share_links"> 
        <li><a rel="nofollow" href="mailto:?body=Thought%20you%20might%20be%20interested%20in%20this%20article%20on%20UCR%20Today%3A%0A%0AWeb%20Security%20Start-up%20Receives%20%241.1%20million%0A%0AStart-up%20co-founded%20by%20UC%20Riverside%20graduate%20and%20professor%20that%20helps%20web%20site%20owners%20prevent%2C%20detect%20and%20recover%20from%20hacker%20attacks%20has%20now%20officially%20launched%0A%0Ahttp%3A%2F%2Fatu.cr%2FAtpxXA&amp;subject=UCR%20Today%3A%20Web%20Security%20Start-up%20Receives%20%241.1%20million" title="E-mail this page to a friend" onclick="javascript:_gaq.push(['_trackEvent','Share','E-mail','3167: Web Security Start-up Receives $1.1 million']);"><img src="http://www.ucr.edu/images/icons/mail.png" height="16" width="16" alt="E-mail this page to a friend" /></a></li> 
        <li><a rel="nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=http%3A%2F%2Fatu.cr%2FAtpxXA&amp;t=UCR%20Today%3A%20Web%20Security%20Start-up%20Receives%20%241.1%20million" title="Share this page on Facebook!" onclick="javascript:_gaq.push(['_trackEvent','Share','Facebook','3167: Web Security Start-up Receives $1.1 million']);" target="_blank"><img src="http://www.ucr.edu/images/icons/facebook.png" height="16" width="16" alt="Share this page on Facebook!" /></a></li> 
        <li><a rel="nofollow" href="https://plusone.google.com/_/+1/confirm?hl=en&amp;url=http%3A%2F%2Fatu.cr%2FAtpxXA&amp;title=UCR%20Today%3A%20Web%20Security%20Start-up%20Receives%20%241.1%20million" title="Publicly recommend on Google!" onclick="javascript:_gaq.push(['_trackEvent','Share','Google +1','3167: Web Security Start-up Receives $1.1 million']);" target="_blank"><img src="http://www.ucr.edu/images/icons/google-plus.png" height="16" width="16" alt="Publicly recommend on Google!" /></a></li> 
        <li><a rel="nofollow" href="http://www.linkedin.com/shareArticle?mini=true&amp;source=UC%20Riverside&amp;url=http%3A%2F%2Fatu.cr%2FAtpxXA&amp;title=UCR%20Today%3A%20Web%20Security%20Start-up%20Receives%20%241.1%20million" title="Add this page to LinkedIn!" onclick="javascript:_gaq.push(['_trackEvent','Share','LinkedIn','3167: Web Security Start-up Receives $1.1 million']);" target="_blank"><img src="http://www.ucr.edu/images/icons/linkedin.png" height="16" width="16" alt="Add this page to LinkedIn!" /></a></li> 
        <li><a rel="nofollow" href="http://twitter.com/home?status=%23UCRiverside%3A%20Web%20Security%20Start-up%20Receives%20%241.1%20million%20http%3A%2F%2Fatu.cr%2FAtpxXA" title="Share on Twitter!" onclick="javascript:_gaq.push(['_trackEvent','Share','Twitter','3167: Web Security Start-up Receives $1.1 million']);" target="_blank"><img src="http://www.ucr.edu/images/icons/twitter.png" height="16" width="16" alt="Share on Twitter!" /></a></li> 
        <li><a rel="nofollow" href="javascript:window.print()" title="Print this page" onclick="javascript:_gaq.push(['_trackEvent','Share','Print','3167: Web Security Start-up Receives $1.1 million']);"><img src="http://www.ucr.edu/images/icons/printer.png" height="16" width="16" alt="Print this page" /></a></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div>
      <p>RIVERSIDE, Calif. (<a href="http://www.ucr.edu">www.ucr.edu</a>) — A technology start-up created by a graduate of the University of California, Riverside <a href="http://www.engr.ucr.edu/" onclick="javascript:_gaq.push(['_trackEvent','outbound-article','http://www.engr.ucr.edu/']);">Bourns College of Engineering </a>that focuses on helping web site owners prevent, detect and recover from hacker attacks has raised $1.1 million to expand operations.</p> 
      <p>The money will allow <a href="http://www.stopthehacker.com/" onclick="javascript:_gaq.push(['_trackEvent','outbound-article','http://www.stopthehacker.com/']);">StopTheHacker</a>, which was co-founded by Anirban Banerjee shortly after receiving his Ph.D. from UC Riverside in 2008, to move solely from research and development into selling and marketing its product while continuing to develop new features.</p> 
      <p>“The timing is perfect,” Banerjee said. “The demand for web site security services is exploding and we are perfectly aligned to take advantage of that.”</p> 
      <div id="attachment_3206" class="wp-caption alignright" style="width: 356px">
       <a href="http://ucrtoday.ucr.edu/3167/anirban-banerjee-stopthehacker" rel="attachment wp-att-3206"><img class="size-medium wp-image-3206 " title="Anirban Banerjee" src="http://ucrtoday.ucr.edu/wp-content/uploads/2012/02/anirban-banerjee-stopthehacker-356x267.jpg" alt="Anirban Banerjee" width="356" height="267" /></a>
       <p class="wp-caption-text">Anirban Banerjee, co-founder of StopTheHacker and a UC Riverside graduate</p>
      </div> 
      <p>The numbers back that up. In 2009, the company had two partners. Today, it has seven, including several large web site hosting businesses such as Parallels and Host Europe Group, which hosts about 1 million web sites. It is also in talks with about 20 more, including five that host more than 1 million web sites.</p> 
      <p>Demand for the services offered by StopTheHacker is driven in large part by Google removing sites that contain malicious code implanted by hackers from its search results. An analysis by StopTheHacker found 6,000 sites are removed, or blacklisted, each day by Google.</p> 
      <p>Being victimized can have a large impact on revenue and reputation. For example, in January, online retailer Zappos asked its 24 million customers to reset their passwords after being victimized by a cyberattack.</p> 
      <p>StopTheHacker, which was based in Riverside until moving to San Francisco last year, is different than other web site security applications in that it uses artificial intelligence algorithms to detect malware. Other providers use signature, or database, solutions that are not as effective.</p> 
      <p>StopTheHacker.com’s advantage is that it is non-intrusive because it is offered on the cloud, meaning users don’t have to install software or change anything beyond what the web site host is doing.</p> 
      <p>StopTheHacker, which is aiming to work with small and medium sized businesses that can’t afford staff devoted to web site security, offers a suite of services, including monitoring web sites for malware, assessing web sites for vulnerabilities and monitoring to see if a web site has been blacklisted.</p> 
      <p>Banerjee, who came to the United States from India in 2004 to pursue his Ph.D. at UC Riverside, co-founded the company with <a href="http://www.engr.ucr.edu/faculty/cs/faloutsos.html" onclick="javascript:_gaq.push(['_trackEvent','outbound-article','http://www.engr.ucr.edu/faculty/cs/faloutsos.html']);">Michalis Faloutsos</a>, a computer science and engineering professor at UC Riverside with whom he studied under.</p> 
      <div id="attachment_3168" class="wp-caption alignright" style="width: 356px">
       <a href="http://ucrtoday.ucr.edu/3167/michalis-001" rel="attachment wp-att-3168"><img class="size-medium wp-image-3168" title="Michalis Faloutsos" src="http://ucrtoday.ucr.edu/wp-content/uploads/2012/02/michalis-001-356x236.jpg" alt="Michalis Faloutsos" width="356" height="236" /></a>
       <p class="wp-caption-text">Michalis Faloutsos, professor of computer science and engineering and co-founder of StopTheHacker</p>
      </div> 
      <p>StopTheHacker also employs two students who received master’s degrees in computer science at the university, Adam Woss and Conley Read. Read works part-time as a consultant.</p> 
      <p>Faloutsos, who has studied web security for 15 years, believes it is following the same trajectory as desktop computer security. Ten years ago, people didn’t think much about desktop security. Today, nearly every desktop has antivirus software.</p> 
      <p>Today, about 10 percent of web sites are protected against malware, software designed to disrupt computer operation. Faloutsos predicts that number will reach 90 percent by 2015.</p> 
      <p>The $1.1 million comes from several private investors, led by Moscow, Russia-based Runa Capital, and the National Science Foundation, which in 2009 and 2010 provided $600,000 in funding from its Small Business Innovative Research grant program.</p> 
      <p>Faloutsos also credits several others with helping StopTheHacker. These people include: Don Dye, the president and CEO of Riverside-based Acorn Technology; Rajan Kassety, CEO and co-founder of Riverside-based Terrafore; and Helen Chen, vice president of business development at Riverside-based Ambryx Biotechnology Inc.</p> 
      <div class="clear"></div>

     <div id="text-3" class="boxed widget widget_text"> 
      <div class="textwidget">
       <div class="shaded"> 
        <h3><img src="/wp-content/uploads/2012/08/ttl_expertsondemand.png" alt="" height="17" width="242" /><span class="accessibility">Experts on Demand</span></h3> 
        <p class="kicker">UC Riverside has dozens of experts in virtually every field you can imagine.</p> 
        <p> Whether it's the latest fad in Hollywood, the latest must-have gadget or the latest row in Washington, UCR has a vast pool of staff and faculty who can present a unique view right now. </p> 
        <p> These interactions can take place in person, electronically, through a campus ISDN line, or even via video through our Digital Production Studio, which can put a UCR expert on the air anywhere in the world through AT&amp;T's regional fiber network hub. </p> 
        <p> UCR is ready to help you find the expertise you need to get the story. </p> 
        <p> <a class="final_link" href="http://mediasources.ucr.edu/">Check out our Experts on Demand</a> </p> 
       </div>
      </div> 
     </div>

  <div class="pagewrapper"> 
   <h3 class="accessibility">Footer</h3> 
   <div id="colophon">
     The University of California, Riverside (
    <a href="http://www.ucr.edu/">www.ucr.edu</a>) is a doctoral research university, a living laboratory for groundbreaking exploration of issues critical to Inland Southern California, the state and communities around the world. Reflecting California's diverse culture, UCR's enrollment has exceeded 21,000 students. The campus opened a medical school in 2013 and has reached the heart of the Coachella Valley by way of the UCR Palm Desert Center. The campus has an annual statewide economic impact of more than $1 billion. A broadcast studio with fiber cable to the AT&amp;T Hollywood hub is available for live or taped interviews. UCR also has ISDN for radio interviews. To learn more, call (951) UCR-NEWS. 
   </div>
